  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_192b736b-b321-4a1e-b5f9-41297cd6577a'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();
    }

She wakes here as a slave, a captive in chains.<br /><br />Sofia's life takes a thrilling and terrifying turn when she is the one selected out of hundreds of girls to join the harem of Derek Novak, the dark royal Prince.<br /><br />Despite his addiction to power and obsessive thirst for her blood, Sofia soon realizes that the safest place on the island is within his quarters, and she must do all within her power to win him over if she is to survive even one more night.<br /><br />Will she succeed? ...or is she destined to the same fate that all other girls have met at the hands of the Novaks?</span>

<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/14319537-katy"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1453736485i/14319537._UX100_CR0,16,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/14319537-katy">Katy</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I was like you and saw all of the hype on Facebook and Amazon about this book. I picked up and read it quickly because it is so short. I was severely <a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I was like you and saw all of the hype on Facebook and Amazon about this book. I picked up and read it quickly because it is so short. I was severely let down after all of the praise it received. I found it rather predictable and boring. I did start the second one in the series thinking that there must be a reason that there are at least nine books in the Shade series, but I could not get myself to finish it. If you are bored and looking for a quick, cheap read, then I saw go for it. If not, then don't bother. That is just my opinion, but clearly there are people out there who enjoyed it. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I can only answer for the 1st book, but it's definitely more along the lines of Twilight than Sookie Stackhouse. It's probably perfect for young adult<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I can only answer for the 1st book, but it's definitely more along the lines of Twilight than Sookie Stackhouse. It's probably perfect for young adult readers, but I expected much more from it with all the hype I kept seeing. I'm unsure if I want to keep reading the rest of the books, it's not a bad book, but I think it was intended for younger readers. There's no sex in this book.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<div id="review_992191860" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/992191860" />
    <a title="Steph Sinclair" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4642710-steph-sinclair"><img alt="Steph Sinclair" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1457555690p2/4642710.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/992191860?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Steph Sinclair" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Steph Sinclair" href="/user/show/4642710-steph-sinclair">Steph Sinclair</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Twihards</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Steph by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/11002017-florentina">Florentina</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=le-sigh">le-sigh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=lol-what">lol-what</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=vamps">vamps</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=2014-reads">2014-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=youve-got-to-be-kidding-me">youve-got-to-be-kidding-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=my-boyfriend-wants-me-dead">my-boyfriend-wants-me-dead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=lots-of-fail-going-on-here">lots-of-fail-going-on-here</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=indies-are-rockstars">indies-are-rockstars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer992191860" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16621623072038921108">I went into this book like a person between jobs, bored of their last venture and not yet ready to dive into anything too serious. I knew exactly what I was getting myself into and my expectations were appropriately set for mindless entertainment. I know this may seem like a strange thing for some people and I'm sure many would wonder why I decided to read a book I was sure to dislike. The simple explanation would lie somewhere between "Because I felt like it" and "Because I paid for it." But fo</span>
  <span id="freeText16621623072038921108" style="display:none">I went into this book like a person between jobs, bored of their last venture and not yet ready to dive into anything too serious. I knew exactly what I was getting myself into and my expectations were appropriately set for mindless entertainment. I know this may seem like a strange thing for some people and I'm sure many would wonder why I decided to read a book I was sure to dislike. The simple explanation would lie somewhere between "Because I felt like it" and "Because I paid for it." But for those of you who aren't as easily pacified, I'll say this: Reading books like this is like inviting your friends over for a night of popcorn, ice cream and really, really terrible horror movies. It takes itself so seriously, that you can't take <em>it</em> seriously. And instead of scaring you, the intentional outcome, it has the reverse effect, providing you and your friends endless fodder for punch lines to new jokes and puns equally as terrible as its source material.<br><br>But the moral question, of course, must be considered. <em>Is this fair to the author?</em> And to that I would have to reply in the affirmative and point such cynics in the direction of my Amazon receipt. <em>A Shade of Vampire</em> isn't a book that I would recommend or even one that I could see myself coming back to. It's served it's purpose of being different enough from what I usually read, breaking up the monotony. It entertained me and now I shall entertain you. (Also, spoiler alert.)<br><br>Here we go.<br><br><em>Twilight</em>.<br><br>There. I've already shot, mangled and killed the Fat Elephant in the room right out the gate. I'm not pulling the "T" card strictly because this book is about vampires and forbidden love. Plenty of other Paranormal Romance books have those qualities and still maintain their independence from the pop culture phenomenon. I bring it up because it's inevitable and follows similar book canon. As such, I created a Choose Your Own Adventure based on <em>A Shade of Vampire</em>.<br><br><strong>Choose Your Own Adventure: <em>A Shade of Vampire</em><br></strong><br><br><strong>1.</strong> You're walking through the park alone, feeling down and under appreciated by family and friends. A handsome stranger comes out of nowhere. He's creepy, invades your space and asks you name. You:<br><br><strong>A.</strong> Tell him your name and force yourself not to run away because you'll show your friends and family! So what if he turns out to be some psycho serial killer. You're 16 and invincible and living on the wild side for once. WHOO-HOOO! YEAH BABY!  (Proceed to #2)<br><br><strong>B.</strong> Run, because he could be some psycho serial killer. (Proceed to #6)<br><br> <br><br><strong>2.</strong> Okay, so that was totally not smart and now you're tied up to a post in a basement. Turns out they want to pamper, primp and prime you for this important Vampire Prince. You vow to be smart from now on about your decisions. You are brought before the Prince along with several other girls, made up for the sole purpose of sexual objectification. You're scared and nervous, so you hold one of the other girl's hands. The Prince notices this gesture and singles you out! Oh noz! He slams you against the wall hard, ready to suck you dry. You:<br><br><strong>A.</strong> Tell yourself you are not the victim here, despite clearly being in a victim-like situation. It's something your Yoda, best friend used to always tell you. So naturally you tell the Prince, who just can't seem to control his thirst even though he really, really wants to, that he is also not a victim.  You do all this with a clear head even though Vampire Fangs are breaths away from your throat. Also, you are a Mary Sue. (Proceed to #3)<br><br><strong>B.</strong> Think about the great life you had and go down fighting like the lion you are. You die. <strong>GAME OVER.</strong><br><br> <br><br><strong>3.</strong> Whew! Somehow that worked! Who knew your Yoda best friend's advice could come in handy against a Vampire Prince with a tortured past?! As a result, the Prince has taking a liking to you and gives you the plush room right next to his in his pimped out tree house (because where else would a vampire sleep? A coffin? Yeah, right). In fact, he's drawn to you and you to him. But you have to get home, so when the Prince thinks you're sleeping, you:<br><br><strong>A.</strong> Miraculously find a hoodie and pair of shorts in your closet that's conveniently filled with cocktail dresses, find a way down the treehouse, and make a run for it... all on the same page! Who needs details? You have no idea where you're going, but you'll find a way. You're the heroine after all! (Proceed to #4)<br><br><strong>B.</strong> Buy out the opportune time. You get to know the Prince and find out as much as you can about the secluded town to help plot your escape. All things come to those who are smart. (Proceed to #6)<br><br> <br><br><strong>4.</strong> This was a bad idea. You didn't realize this was an island with no way of escape! WAAAA WAAA! They even have a fence as tall as the wall of China! UGH. Damn Vamps! If only you had attempted to learn more about this place, maybe you could have anticipated this and prepared better. Alas, you are a dunderhead. Oh, no! Here come two guards. You:<br><br><strong>A.</strong> Think about name-dropping your powerful master's name in the hopes that it'll put fear into their hearts, but you allow yourself to be interrupted because something has to encourage this ridiculous plot along. This is it. Your death is coming. (Proceed to #5)<br><br><strong>B.</strong> Run. You Die. <strong>GAME OVER</strong>, silly girl.<br><br> <br><br><strong>5.</strong> One of the guards has his fangs in your neck. Just as you are mentally saying goodbye to your life, the Vampire Prince comes out of nowhere and rips you away from the attackers. Then some serious Indiana Jones type shit happens.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406831633ra/10604248.gif" alt="heart-rip-o" width="320" height="240" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You're scared, hurt and mentally cursing yourself for yet another terrible decision. Vampire Prince makes you drink his blood to heal yourself and takes you back to your fancy prison. He tells you never to run away again and that you are his. You:<br><br><strong>Fall in love because he seems like a nice guy underneath it all. GAME OVER.</strong><br><br> <br><br><strong>6.</strong> Congrats! You're probably not a dunderhead, but will most likely still die because you're playing by cliché YA rules. May the odds be ever in your favor.<br><br> <br><br>The basic plot for <em>A Shade of Vampire</em> is Sofia coming to accept Derek and help heal him. I'm generally not a fan of those type of books because it creates an imbalance in the relationship and breeds co-dependence. The next thing you know the characters are proclaiming their undying love and saying things like they'll never love another or how they can't be without that person. Of course, you also have the fact that Derek wants to EAT Sofia. And somehow after 400 years of not drinking blood, he's able to resist Sofia because she's different.<br><blockquote>No other woman -- and believe me when I say that I've been with many -- had the same effect that Sofia Claremont has on me. [...] She'd only recently entered my life, yet it felt like I'd known her for ages.</blockquote><br>OH REALLY?<br><blockquote>I've already stopped even thinking about a life that doesn't have Derek Novak in it.<br><br>Whether I liked it or not, home had become wherever Derek Novak was.</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406831633ra/10604249.gif" alt="jim carrey gag" width="300" height="225" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What made me angry was the not so subtle sexism and slut shaming that went on. Sofia is a member of Prince Derek's harem and other Vamps in the town assume she's sleeping with him, because HAREM, and all that. Sofia is oblivious to this until a member of the Prince's guard says she's doing a good job of pleasing him. And she replies:<br><blockquote>"That's not... I would never!" I spluttered.<br>Here I was, a virgin, being rumored to have given the newly awakened prince a pleasurable night in bed.<br>He frowned, an amused glint in the corners of his eyes. "You mean you didn't..."<br>My eyes widened. "No! I'm not that kind of girl..."</blockquote><br>Then we have Derek's brother, Lucas, who wants nothing more than to rape and kill Sofia. Every time he showed up in a scene he made these intentions clear. Because it's not enough that he wanted to drink her blood and kill her, he has to want to rape her too.<br><blockquote>The lust was unmistakable. He was practically undressing her with those eyes and I could tell that Sofia felt it based on how she sat there tense and unmoving.</blockquote><br>But why does Lucas want Sofia so bad? WHAT'S HIS MOTIVATION? Her blood smells good just wasn't a good enough for me. But that brings us to the novel's biggest issue. Regardless of the clichés, <em>A Shade of Vampire</em> could have been decent if the writing had been tighter and not had sentences like this:<br><blockquote>I was aware of it all, and yet, I wasn't. It was almost like everything was happening to another person, and yet it was me.</blockquote><br>WUT. Let me help you: "It was surreal."<br><br>The characters could have also used some development besides the usual descriptions. Sofia is a girl who can do no wrong, a pure virgin, The One to Change Derek, selfless, not used to attention, etc. The only unique thing about her is her Low Latent Inhibition disorder, which basically amounts to nothing more than a really good memory. I kept wondering if it would somehow relate to the plot or have some other use, but it's kinda like Nora's iron pills from <em>Hush, Hush</em>. They serve no other purpose than being present.<br><br>(OH. And there just happens to be a witch on the vampire island who also was a psychologist and able to diagnose this disorder. I swear this book was written with an Easy Button.)<br><br>The underlying plot with the war between the other covens and Vampire Hunters would have been more interesting if it had more page time instead of just being casually mentioned once or twice. This is certainly not the worst book I've ever read, but I can't really recommend it to anyone either unless you're bored or a huge <em>Twilight</em>/<em>Hush, Hush</em> fan. And even then, this book may be too ridiculous to be true.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16621623072038921108" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer616449293" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18077685967756013047">This book has a lot of mixed reviews from being compared to Twilight to people saying it's amazing.<br/><br/>So I was like;<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421738ra/838240.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Big mistake there!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421738ra/838241.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Yeah, I was an idiot for wasting time and money on this. <b>Another fucking insta-love</b>, and believe me when I say it's an annoying one, because I can stand certain amount of insta-cheesy-love. But this was just absurd, throw that in a bowl, add some poor writing, and you are up for a very shitty novel.<br/><br/><b>Some examples:</b><br/><br/><i>"I caught <b>myself</b> before I could turn <b>myself</b> into my own</i></span>
  <span id="freeText18077685967756013047" style="display:none">This book has a lot of mixed reviews from being compared to Twilight to people saying it's amazing.<br><br>So I was like;<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421738ra/838240.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Big mistake there!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421738ra/838241.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yeah, I was an idiot for wasting time and money on this. <b>Another fucking insta-love</b>, and believe me when I say it's an annoying one, because I can stand certain amount of insta-cheesy-love. But this was just absurd, throw that in a bowl, add some poor writing, and you are up for a very shitty novel.<br><br><b>Some examples:</b><br><br><i>"I caught <b>myself</b> before I could turn <b>myself</b> into my own personal villain. The severity of the situation hit me full force and I was unable to suppress a shudder. What have I gotten <b>myself</b> into?"</i><br><br><i>"Contemptuous that I would <b>wake</b> when I so explicitly asked to be given an escape from which I would never <b>wake</b>..."</i><br><br><i>"I was still marveling at the <b>places</b> we were passing by when they ushered us to a <b>place</b> that..."</i><br><br><b>Um, repetitive much?</b> Somebody let the author know about the use of synonyms ASAP please. <br><br><u>And those were extracted from only 15% of the book.</u><br><br>I do have to agree with my peeps here saying that this is like Twilight. I mean, the guy is a tortured vampire... <i>Oh, I'm so beautiful, and powerful, and immortal... Please kill me.</i> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/580463.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the girl, <b>she is convinced that she is plain and boring</b>, but guess what? Yep, the powerful gorgeous vampire dude can't stay away from her. <i>Because fuck it.</i> She is also very naive (or very stupid), she is kidnapped and while at it she thinks this:<br><br><i>"Everything about him told me that I wasn’t safe around him. His next actions solidified my suspicions that his intentions toward me were less than noble."</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/488218.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Oh, and here was I thinking that kidnappers were good people.</b> I mean, what. the. heck. You are being held against your will. One would think that is enough reason to know the guy has no good intention.<br><br>About the "vampire world" that is contemplated here, I didn't find it amusing or interesting in any way. I only read a bunch of supernatural buddies living in a coven protected by knights(?) and collected Harems.<br><br>I read about 30% of the book, and honestly that was enough between all the cheese and the meager storytelling.<br><br><i>Needless to say,</i> <b>I dont recommend it at all.</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="18077685967756013047" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer616248610" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2584122623408233727"><b>WHAT THE...?<br/>WHAT THE HECK...?!<br/>WHAT THE HECK JUST HAPPENED?!!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://postimage.org/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421708ra/838138.gif' alt='tumblr m2lcqr7 QJf1qihztbo1 500 zps8fe0ce4a' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://postimage.org/app.php' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>Errmm, i think it's illegal to end a book like that. You juts can't do that, OK?</b><br/><br/><i>Sophia is kidnapped at her 17th birthday. She's taken captive by a vampire to an island where the sun never shines. <br/>The island is called The Shade.<a href='http://postimage.org/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421708i/838139.jpg' alt='11c57561 169b 47c4 8609 ec9d54b9869c zpsf69aaea5' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://postimage.org/app.php' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/><br/> Sofia is selected out of hundreds of girls to join the harem of Derek Novak, the dark royal Prince. Sofia soon realises that if she's to survive she must gain Derek's affection. But will she? And what will </i></span>
  <span id="freeText2584122623408233727" style="display:none"><b>WHAT THE...?<br>WHAT THE HECK...?!<br>WHAT THE HECK JUST HAPPENED?!!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421708ra/838138.gif" alt="tumblr m2lcqr7 QJf1qihztbo1 500 zps8fe0ce4a" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b>Errmm, i think it's illegal to end a book like that. You juts can't do that, OK?</b><br><br><i>Sophia is kidnapped at her 17th birthday. She's taken captive by a vampire to an island where the sun never shines. <br>The island is called The Shade.<a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421708i/838139.jpg" alt="11c57561 169b 47c4 8609 ec9d54b9869c zpsf69aaea5" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br> Sofia is selected out of hundreds of girls to join the harem of Derek Novak, the dark royal Prince. Sofia soon realises that if she's to survive she must gain Derek's affection. But will she? And what will happen if the feeling will become mutual? </i><br><br>When i read through some 'bad' and 'good' reviews about this book i heard it's a copy version of twilight. <a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421708ra/838140.gif" alt="tumblr m6sczos YEN1qac2a8 zpsb33bd18f" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br> Now listen. Just because this book is about vampires and they're pale doesn't freaking mean this is like twilight! God! Why do you people think everything is copied from twilight?! Just stop! Twilight is like 1 million years old. <b>GET A FREAKING MOVE ON!</b> <br> <br>Anyways...<br><br><b>Meet the main characters!</b> <br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421708i/838141.jpg" alt="65445b07 1ac3 47cf b5c9 e89e2631e5b8 zps28dfbeb2" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"> </a><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421708i/838142.jpg" alt="660132a3 c846 47d2 8791 2ed69bc22f0c zpsee969453" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br> <br><i>
  <u>What i thought about Sofia?:</u>
</i> The first few pages i didn't really like her, mainly because of this - <blockquote>
  <b>....determined to start having fun again with the most important person in my life, but then i'd remember... I'd remember what it felt like to see him with his arms around Tanya Wilson.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Now, if you don't know, she's talking here about her BFF Ben that she has a crush on and beliefs to be her 'the one and only'. When i first read that paragraph i was like <br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421708ra/838143.gif" alt="tumblr ma5lgk LFDl1r2ej51 zps5abe813a" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><b>NOT.AGAIN!</b> Girl falling for her best friend? Sound similar? But, her feelings did start to change when she spent more time with Derek, slowly growing feelings for him in the process. She was also a strong character who didn't like to be told what to do. That's what i loved about her the most! <br><br><i>
  <u>What i thought about Derek?:</u>
</i> I absolutely <b>LOVE</b> him! Since the moment i met him he stole my heart. He's the strongest vampire in the world. Who doesn't like muscular/ strong physically hotties!? I do! But Derek is also smart, inspiring, full of potential and very loyal to people he loves. He is bossy, i mean c'mon! He's a freaking prince! Aren't all of them like that? But he learns to respect others, mainly Sofias, opinions and will.<a href="http://myniceprofile.com/love-22464.html" title="Love Comments Pictures" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421708ra/838144.gif" alt="Love Comments Pictures" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://myniceprofile.com/" title="Love Comments Pictures" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br>I really loved this book. I couldn't put it down. It's my fav of the month so far! The writing style really pulls you in, and the characters just make you <i>care</i> about what's happening. <br><br>The book wastes no time. It starts of when Sofia get's captured, and i'm thankful for that. At least there are no 200 pages just dragging on about particularly nothing, and yes, i'm talking especially about you <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6304335.Beautiful_Creatures__Caster_Chronicles___1_" title="Beautiful Creatures (Caster Chronicles, #1) by Kami Garcia" rel="nofollow noopener">Beautiful Creatures</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12157365.Unraveling__Unraveling___1_" title="Unraveling (Unraveling, #1) by Elizabeth Norris" rel="nofollow noopener">Unraveling</a>. <br><br>The ending was a bit let down to be honest. Sofia was unbelievable. I don't think i have ever wanted to shake and strangle a character this bad. She was so mean to Derek! She would like literally ditch him the moment he says "you're free to go". Ahhh! <br><a href="http://s1296.photobucket.com/user/booksandpoemsxxx/media/tumblr_mjz4ydMlCq1s4sar6o1_500_zpsa26ea6c2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421708ra/838145.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mjz4ydMlCq1s4sar6o1_500_zpsa26ea6c2.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://s1296.photobucket.com/user/booksandpoemsxxx/media/tumblr_mi2mjp3xbz1s3lzifo1_500_large_zpsac5e0fb9-1_zpsdfd0e483.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421708ra/838146.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mi2mjp3xbz1s3lzifo1_500_large_zpsac5e0fb9-1_zpsdfd0e483.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><b>Overall</b> <i>A Shade of Vampire</i> was an extremely entertaining book that i stayed up late for because i couldn't put it down. The creative vampire world and awesome characters were great! I have to read book 2 ASAP! Definitely recommend this to everyone! :)<br><br><b>Thank you Bella Forrest for providing me an ARC copy! It was a pleasure!! &lt;3</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2584122623408233727" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=paranormal-fantasy">paranormal-fantasy</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer586510721" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15823067062792212617">I waited so long to read A Shade of Vampire and it was worth the wait. It was short but the pages were packed with so much. Bella paints such a vivid picture of the island of The Shade that serves as a refuge for a coven of vampires, led by their prince, Derek Novak. Derek's very evil brother, Lucas, kidnaps Sofia and brings her to The Shade for Derek's harem but secretly wants Sofia for himself. This book is packed with just the right combination of evil and romance. You can't help but fall for</span>
  <span id="freeText15823067062792212617" style="display:none">I waited so long to read A Shade of Vampire and it was worth the wait. It was short but the pages were packed with so much. Bella paints such a vivid picture of the island of The Shade that serves as a refuge for a coven of vampires, led by their prince, Derek Novak. Derek's very evil brother, Lucas, kidnaps Sofia and brings her to The Shade for Derek's harem but secretly wants Sofia for himself. This book is packed with just the right combination of evil and romance. You can't help but fall for Derek right along with Sofia and let me tell you, there are plenty of awesome one-liners in this book that melted my heart. I am a sucker for a good vampire romance and this didn't let me down. Can't wait for the next book which I will start in about 5 minutes. Thank you Bella Forrest. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15823067062792212617" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2775476683" />
    <a title="Nazanin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39893246-nazanin"><img alt="Nazanin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600407709p2/39893246.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer16998408890232755220"><b>4 Stars</b><br/><br/>Told in dual POV, 1st person. It’s cliffy with very short chapters. It’s the first installment in the (veeeeerrryyyy loooong) "A Shade of Vampire" series (it contains 75 books so far). I don’t know if I'll read all of them but this is a good start to the series.   <span id="freeText16998408890232755220" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars</b><br /><br />Told in dual POV, 1st person. It’s cliffy with very short chapters. It’s the first installment in the (veeeeerrryyyy loooong) "A Shade of Vampire" series (it contains 75 books so far). I don’t know if I'll read all of them but this is a good start to the series. My issue was that Sofia was too much cool for someone who was kidnapped with night creatures at the age of seventeen! And when she was kidnapped, she didn’t think of her father or other people, that whether they were going to search for her or not! Another thing is we knew very little about Vampires in this world. Overall, it was an enjoyable read and hope you like it as well!</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1577765327?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" href="/user/show/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin">Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17255372-a-shade-of-vampire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin?shelf=fantasy-all">fantasy-all</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1577765327" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3768352795003032495">MY BLOG: <a href='http://melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com/2016/03/a-shade-of-vampire-by-bella-forrest.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Melissa Martin's Reading List</a><br/><br/>I have been wanting to start reading this series for some time and damn it, I decided today was the day. <br/><br/>I love Sofia and Derek together! I really liked this book and I look forward to the rest of them! Yay! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457829068i/18411453._SY540_.jpg' alt=' : ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454034089i/17907377._SX540_.jpg' alt=' : ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Sofia is living with the Hudson family. They were friends with her mother, Camilla, and her father. But, Sofia's mom was a little whackadoo there for a bit and got put away and then her father just dumped her on this family. I really wonder though if som</span>
  <span id="freeText3768352795003032495" style="display:none">MY BLOG: <a href="http://melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com/2016/03/a-shade-of-vampire-by-bella-forrest.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Melissa Martin's Reading List</a><br><br>I have been wanting to start reading this series for some time and damn it, I decided today was the day. <br><br>I love Sofia and Derek together! I really liked this book and I look forward to the rest of them! Yay! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457829068i/18411453._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454034089i/17907377._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sofia is living with the Hudson family. They were friends with her mother, Camilla, and her father. But, Sofia's mom was a little whackadoo there for a bit and got put away and then her father just dumped her on this family. I really wonder though if something is going to come up about her mother later on. Anyhoo, so there are two other children in the home that are the actual kids of the family. There is little Abigail and Ben, Ben is Sofia's age and her best friend. And... she has a crush on him. I think this only came about when he became the only person that could calm her panic attacks and such. But... there is always a but... Ben seems to have a lot of girlfriends, not all at once, but he's a football player (so what) and all the girls want him. <br><br>One night when the family goes on vacation together Sofia decides she's going to tell Ben her real feelings when one of his exes comes along and ruins it. Ben says he's going to spend three nights that the ex has left with her and he misses Sofia's bday. I'm not sure what parents just lets their son go off and spend three days with some chic, but I digress. When Ben tries to apologize, Sofia runs off to the beach at night to be a lone for awhile. On her way back she gets snagged by this jerk named Lucas. She wakes up on an island called the Shade that belongs to vampires. She is going to be one of the slaves to the prince when he awakens. Well... when he awakens.. things don't go quite as his brother Lucas (jerk) or sister Vivienne plan. Derek has a bond with Sofia because she shows him kindness before he is about to eat her and thus he is intrigued with this. I mean he's been asleep for 400 years ---&gt;long story, read the book. <br><br>Anyway, they live on this island and live in these awesome tree houses! Yes!! Tree houses! I love me some tree houses. Theirs is all decked out as you can imagine.. um.. no pun intended there. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457829068i/18411454.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Derek is actually nice to all of the girls they brought to him only because of Sofia. So they don't have to worry about getting eaten unless some arse sneaks into Derek's home and eats them, he has guards but they can be knocked out. Some of those parts I don't understand. <br><br>Anyway, Sofia seems to slowly be falling in love with Derek because of his kindness and he's just different, he doesn't push her to do things. Now, his crap arse brother on the other hand keeps trying to get her. Just kill him someone, damn. Okay, so there is a moment Sofia talks Derek out of killing him so he wouldn't be upset about it. My arse! I would have been cheering him on, but that's just me! <br><br>I don't want to give much more away, but Ben ends up showing up. Like really, lets just leave him out of it for awhile. <br><br>There are some politics that are involved as Derek has to find out a way to keep the vampires safe from hunters and other crap going on. I liked the way the book ended and am looking forward to the next book. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3768352795003032495" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <i>Yes, we like our fluffy young adult vampire romances! </i>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1745808390" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8786364177949856427">Find all of my reviews at: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/'>http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br/><br/>My friend <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1689150176?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sh3lly</a> was reading this series awhile back and her updates were all shades of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1223768152?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twilight</a>. . . . <br/><br/><a href='http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473186364ra/20423769.gif' alt='commercial photography locations' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Don’t judge. <br/><br/>Anyway, I figured what the hell. She was even nice enough to attempt to lend me a copy but there was a glitch in the system somewhere because <s>I suck at technology</s> the universe is out to get me. Lucky for me the porny librarian is also versed in all things vampire and my turn came up at <b>exactly</b> the right time for mind</span>
  <span id="freeText8786364177949856427" style="display:none">Find all of my reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/">http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br><br>My friend <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1689150176?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Sh3lly</a> was reading this series awhile back and her updates were all shades of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1223768152?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Twilight</a>. . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473186364ra/20423769.gif" alt="commercial photography locations" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Don’t judge. <br><br>Anyway, I figured what the hell. She was even nice enough to attempt to lend me a copy but there was a glitch in the system somewhere because <s>I suck at technology</s> the universe is out to get me. Lucky for me the porny librarian is also versed in all things vampire and my turn came up at <b>exactly</b> the right time for mindless fluff – a holiday weekend.<br><br>I was sooooooo ready to get my fang on. Unfortunately, this wasn’t the one for me. I know what you’re all thinking . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473186364ra/20423770.gif" alt="commercial photography locations" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>You are 100% right so don’t bother trolling me. I’ve read enough vampire books to know that . . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473186364ra/20423771.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And I’ll still probably eat it right up. As stated before, I was expecting a bit of a <i>Twilight</i> knock-off so I never imagined I would dislike this so much. Things that I’m apparently okay with? 117 year old creepers who like to watch high school girls while they sleep. Things that I’m not okay with? Girls who get dissed and dismissed on their own effing birthday when their bestie/crush decides to make smush smush with some other chick who then get kidnapped on a rando Mexican beach and have the following reaction . . . <br><br><b>
  <i>“My last thought was that I might never see Ben again.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473186364ra/20423772.gif" alt="commercial photography locations" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Have no fear, though, it only took an escape attempt and a couple of hot minutes before she went all instalove on her new captor. And <b>of course</b> that’s the moment that Ben came back into the picture. Meaning #2 will probably be all . . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473186364ra/20423773.gif" alt="commercial photography locations" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Or Sophia. Tomato tomahto. <br><br>Nothing about this worked for me. I have no clue how old the author is, but the writing seemed <b>very</b> young – like a child might have written it. The characters were all pretty cardboard and due to this being a serial the story progression was nearly non-existent. It’s now come to my attention that there are <b>THIRTY-THREE</b> novellas in this collection, to which I say . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473186364ra/20423774.gif" alt="commercial photography locations" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>No way. No how.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8786364177949856427" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_742325840" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/742325840" />
    <a title="Courtney Wells" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19433724-courtney-wells"><img alt="Courtney Wells" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1392617868p2/19433724.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/742325840?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Courtney Wells" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Courtney Wells" href="/user/show/19433724-courtney-wells">Courtney Wells</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19433724-courtney-wells?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer742325840" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5318151231055143014">Before I begin, I feel the need to quantify my five-stars here. You know how people will say something is "so bad it's good"? I feel that term somewhat applies here, though more in a sense "It's a great read, if you like that sort of thing". <br/><br/>As such, <i>A Shade of Vampire</i> is a "great read" if you like swooning human heroines and smoldering love-interests with fangs. For those who aren't fans of those tired cliches, know you're not getting a new experience here. Otherwise - for those who partake in </span>
  <span id="freeText5318151231055143014" style="display:none">Before I begin, I feel the need to quantify my five-stars here. You know how people will say something is "so bad it's good"? I feel that term somewhat applies here, though more in a sense "It's a great read, if you like that sort of thing". <br /><br />As such, <i>A Shade of Vampire</i> is a "great read" if you like swooning human heroines and smoldering love-interests with fangs. For those who aren't fans of those tired cliches, know you're not getting a new experience here. Otherwise - for those who partake in the occasional guilty pleasure - this should scratch an itch for you.<br /><br /><i>A Shade of Vampire</i> is the first novel in a series that seems capable of satisfying those who were charmed by the chaste, boy-met-girl romance <i>Twilight</i> offered readers while incorporating darker, more sultry elements that entice viewers into shows like <i>The Vampire Diaries</i>. That's not to say it's a knock-off of either, per se, but it does draw from such sources to give readers who are fans of the vampire genre familiarity while offering originality and establishing a world of its own.<br /><br /><i>A Shade of Vampire</i> is about 150 pages long, which made it a short read and a good example of what readers can expect of the series. It's a perfect way to get introduced without feeling like you're committing a lot of time and see if you're intrigued by what's being set up. It's worth a try if you're nostalgic for <i>Twilight</i>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5318151231055143014" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_552268295" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/552268295" />
    <a title="Jeann (Happy Indulgence) " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6186603-jeann-happy-indulgence"><img alt="Jeann (Happy Indulgence) " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559561558p2/6186603.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/552268295?book_show_action=true">Mar 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jeann (Happy Indulgence) " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jeann (Happy Indulgence) " href="/user/show/6186603-jeann-happy-indulgence">Jeann (Happy Indulgence) </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6186603-jeann-happy-indulgence?shelf=review-copy">review-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6186603-jeann-happy-indulgence?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6186603-jeann-happy-indulgence?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer552268295" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer820142949978637195">In case you’re wondering, A Shade of Vampire is not just another average vampire book. It’s a quick, captivating read about a 17 year old teenager called Sofia Claremont, who gets captured to an island called The Shade. The island is controlled by vampires who capture humans as slaves and food to do their bidding, and there’s no escape. Sofia is one of several teenage girls who have been caught to serve Derek, a revered and powerful vampire who has just awoken. Despite the terrifying circumstanc</span>
  <span id="freeText820142949978637195" style="display:none">In case you’re wondering, A Shade of Vampire is not just another average vampire book. It’s a quick, captivating read about a 17 year old teenager called Sofia Claremont, who gets captured to an island called The Shade. The island is controlled by vampires who capture humans as slaves and food to do their bidding, and there’s no escape. Sofia is one of several teenage girls who have been caught to serve Derek, a revered and powerful vampire who has just awoken. Despite the terrifying circumstances, both vampire and human develop feelings for each other.<br /><br />This is a relatively short read, told from the perspectives of Derek and Sofia and it quickly covers the event of her capture and how they develop feelings for each other. There’s also the threat of Lucas, Derek’s brother who wants a piece of Sofia which makes things terrifying.<br /><br />Sofia is a fascinating character, highly attuned to her surroundings. She has some reservations about her feelings for a vampire, and rightly so. In contrast, Derek falls quickly for Sofia based on her beauty and care for others, and I sort of felt that his insta-love was a bit creepy in a way. Luckily these feelings subsided when Sofia began to return his feelings.<br /><br />In just 147 words, Bella Forrest fleshes out the circumstances between different characters and we’re left hankering for more. I wanted to know what Derek had done in his life to deserve so much respect and power from everyone, and why he seems to have a shred of humanity intact. I wanted to know more about the conflict between him and Lucas, who posed a threat to Sofia. I also wanted to hear more about Sofia’s ‘best friend’ that she has feelings for, Ben, and whether he felt the same way.<br /><br />Luckily there’s a sequel coming out which will hopefully delve a bit more into my questions. I can’t wait to read the sequel!<br /><br />I received a review copy from the author in exchange for an honest review. Thank you so much, I look forward to reading more of your work.<br /><br />This review has been cross-posted on my <a href="http://happyindulgence.wordpress.com/2013/03/16/a-shade-of-vampire-by-bella-forrest-review/" rel="nofollow noopener">Happy Indulgence</a> blog. Check it out for more reviews!</span>
  <a data-text-id="820142949978637195" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3072315879303610277">A Shade of Vampire (A Shade of Vampire, #1), Bella Forrest<br/><br/>On the evening of <b>Sofia Claremont’s</b> seventeenth birthday, she is sucked into a nightmare from which she cannot wake. A quiet evening walk along a beach brings her face to face with a dangerous pale creature that craves much more than her blood.<br/><br/>She is kidnapped to The Shade, an enchanted island where the sun is eternally forbidden to shine – an island uncharted by any map and ruled by the most powerful vampire coven on the planet. She wake</span>
  <span id="freeText3072315879303610277" style="display:none">A Shade of Vampire (A Shade of Vampire, #1), Bella Forrest<br /><br />On the evening of <b>Sofia Claremont’s</b> seventeenth birthday, she is sucked into a nightmare from which she cannot wake. A quiet evening walk along a beach brings her face to face with a dangerous pale creature that craves much more than her blood.<br /><br />She is kidnapped to The Shade, an enchanted island where the sun is eternally forbidden to shine – an island uncharted by any map and ruled by the most powerful vampire coven on the planet. She wakes here as a slave, a captive in chains.<br /><br />Sofia’s life takes a thrilling and terrifying turn when she is selected out of hundreds of girls to take up residence in the tree-top harem of Derek Novak, the dark royal prince.<br /><br />Despite his addiction to power and obsessive thirst for her blood, Sofia soon realizes that the safest place on the island is within his quarters, and she must do all within her power to win him over if she is to survive even one more night.<br /><br />تاریخ خوانش روز چهارم ماه اکتبر سال 2014 میلادی<br /><br />عنوان: سایه ی خون آشام؛ نویسنده: بللا (بلا) فارست؛ مترجم: پرنیان امینی؛<br /><br />سوفیا کلیرمونت (کلارمونت) شب تولدش، درون کابوسی کشیده می‌شود، و نمی‌تواند بیدار شود؛ هنگامیکه در یک عصر آرام، کنار ساحل قدم می‌زند، با جانور رنگ پریده‌ ی خطرناکی، روبرو می‌شود، که عطش بسیاری، به خون او دارد؛ او ربوده شده، و به جزیره‌ ای برده می‌شود، که تابش خورشید تا ابد در آن قدغن است؛ جزیره‌ ای که روی هیچ نقشه‌ ای نیست، و توسط توانمندترین محفل خون آشام‌ها، اداره می‌شود؛ او در آنجا، در قالب یک برده، و گرفتار در غل و زنجیر، بیدار می‌شود؛ زندگی «سوفیا» آنگاه ترسناکتر می‌شود، که از بین صدها دختر، برای پیوستن به حرمسرای «درک نوواک»، شاهزاده‌ ی تاریکی، برگزیده می‌شود؛ علیرغم اعتیاد «نوواک» به قدرت، و تشنگی وسوسه برانگیزش، برای خون او، «سوفیا» خیلی زود می‌فهمد، که امن‌ترین مکان در جزیره، همان خانه‌ ی «درک نواک» است، و او برای اینکه حتی یک شب، بیشتر زنده بماند، باید تمام سعیش را بکند، تا «نواک» را به دست بیاورد؛ آیا سوفیا موفق می‌شود؟…؛ یا او هم به سرنوشت دیگر دخترهایی دچار می‌شود، که در دستان «نواک» اسیر شده بودند؟ ا. شربیانی</span>

<div id="review_652750480" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/652750480" />
    <a title="Miriam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10072078-miriam"><img alt="Miriam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383915365p2/10072078.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/652750480?book_show_action=true">Jun 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miriam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miriam" href="/user/show/10072078-miriam">Miriam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=1-shitty-star">1-shitty-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=weak-heroine">weak-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10072078-miriam?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer652750480" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8744803425250607222"><b>1.5 stars</b><br/><br/><b><i>A Shade of Vampire</i> is an enjoyable, light, extremely short read.</b> is what I would have liked to said but my fingers keep twitching towards <b>Stay away, it's a piece of crap.</b><br/><br/>I couldn't help but point out various grammatical mistakes and the repetition of sentences when they're everywhere. There's only so many times when a person can say, "Welcome to the *insert-place-here*"! It got to a point where I was <i>begging</i> for no more shitty dialogue. Although, this could have been easily fixed if <i>the</i></span>
  <span id="freeText8744803425250607222" style="display:none"><b>1.5 stars</b><br /><br /><b><i>A Shade of Vampire</i> is an enjoyable, light, extremely short read.</b> is what I would have liked to said but my fingers keep twitching towards <b>Stay away, it's a piece of crap.</b><br /><br />I couldn't help but point out various grammatical mistakes and the repetition of sentences when they're everywhere. There's only so many times when a person can say, "Welcome to the *insert-place-here*"! It got to a point where I was <i>begging</i> for no more shitty dialogue. Although, this could have been easily fixed if <i>there was an editor on hand</i>. Or if there was, fire them. They don't know how to do their job.<br /><br />Another negative point for me, was the <i>love-at-first-sight</i> aspect of the book. I think this is what reminded so many people of Twilight. The vampire sees the girl, wants to feed on her blood but somehow manages to stop himself in time because of how <i>special</i> and <i>unique</i> the said girl was.<br /><br /><i>Same old story</i>. So, <i>yes</i>, I <u>didn't</u> like it.<br /><br />The characters themselves were flawed.<br /><br />Sofia was, might I dare say it, a <b>'Mary-Sue'</b>. <br /><br />1. She didn't think she was pretty, even though she was "beautiful".<br />2. She didn't have a single flaw. <i>Not. A. Single. One.</i> I mean, <i>c'mon</i>, I don't believe this...Unless you count being <i>too</i> perfect as a flaw? <br />3. Every single character, including Derek specially, believed her to be a paragon of virtue, strength and hope. They're all overwhelmed with admiration for her.<br /> <br />Ahhh, Derek. The man I hoped to be my new YA love. And expected to be at least mildly threatening/intriguing <b><i>Instead</i>, I got a sap.</b><br /><br /><i>Don't</i> get me wrong, I love romantic guys who are sensitive and caring and devoted. But I counted the number of Derek's almost-declarations of love...and there were <i>a</i> lot. It was sweet at first, then it got unrealistic.<br /><br />And then there was the fact that he had apparently been asleep for five centures. <b>Five. Centuries</b>. That was sometime in the middle 1900s. My parents can't even keep up with the slang and the trends and they were <i>there for most of it!!</i>. Derek's been out of the loop for a while and he sounds just like the bratty teens.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>I was provided an ARC in exchange for an honest review so even though I didn't enjoy it very much, I thank the author for giving me a chance to read it.</i>
</b><br /><br />P.S Was this review too honest?</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_695754048" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/695754048" />
    <a title="Sigourney" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5654896-sigourney"><img alt="Sigourney" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515101928p2/5654896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/695754048?book_show_action=true">Aug 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sigourney" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sigourney" href="/user/show/5654896-sigourney">Sigourney</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5654896-sigourney?shelf=for-review">for-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer695754048" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8220519730394448497"><i>
  <b>A copy of A Shade of Vampire was kindly sent to me by Bella Forrest in exchange for an honest review.</b>
</i> <br/><br/>I really disliked <i>A Shade of Vampire</i>. It seems to me that Forrest has taken a book from the Stephenie Meyer school of writing and followed it exactly. The plot is bland, it’s full of purple prose, the characters are completely unlikable and the heroine made me want to throw things and scream. It manages to be sexist and misogynistic on practically every page – our darling protagonist Sofia i</span>
  <span id="freeText8220519730394448497" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>A copy of A Shade of Vampire was kindly sent to me by Bella Forrest in exchange for an honest review.</b>
</i> <br /><br />I really disliked <i>A Shade of Vampire</i>. It seems to me that Forrest has taken a book from the Stephenie Meyer school of writing and followed it exactly. The plot is bland, it’s full of purple prose, the characters are completely unlikable and the heroine made me want to throw things and scream. It manages to be sexist and misogynistic on practically every page – our darling protagonist Sofia is even <i>flattered</i> about being the property of a blood sucking vamp. You go girl. Derek, said blood sucking vamp, is Edward Cullen incarnate – sulky and remorseful, he even wants a music room. <br /><br />It’s only saving grace is that at its most shallow and superficial, at its most basic level as a teen chick lit vampire thing, it succeeds – it’s readable and easy, and, as long as you don’t even think about analysing anything in it, will not fill you with indignant rage. Tweenie girls who won’t read too much into it will probably love it, as will fans of all things Twilight. Educated twenty three year olds with feminist tendencies and a moral code, however, will not.<br /><br />My stream of consciousness notes when I was reading it are below in a spoiler – if you enjoyed this book or don’t want to be enraged further by its contents I suggest you ignore the next part entirely.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[- Sofia: weak willed woman, seems to think she has no substance without a man. Pathetic, imbecile. Only cares about what men think – Ben, Derek. Ridiculous in every situation, especially when kidnapped by vampires. She doesn’t even <i>try</i> to defend herself. Bland, no personality. All anyone cares about is physical appearance – Derek is pretty so everything’s okay. Okaaaaay.<br /><br />-Enter evil sex pest vampire. YAWN.<br /><br />-Casually throwing around mental health issues for lols – ADHD, OCD, bipolar. Oh yes, it’s <i>extremely</i> funny for the main character to go ‘ha ha I’m probably crazy, look at my laundry list of problems that aren’t going to be expanded on at all’. Slut shaming is also thrown into the mix later on. Fantastic. <br /><br />-No likeable characters. AT ALL. No redeeming features. AT ALL.<br /><br />-Sexist misogynistic bullshit all the way through. I thought this was the 21st century?!<br /><br />-Derek – you’re an asshole. You claim a ‘harem’ of innocent, terrified girls as property but we’re supposed to swoon because you didn’t immediately eat them? Hell no. You’re an evil whiny piece of work.<br /><br />-Sofia and Derek – well, we ALL know where that’s going to go. Stockholm syndrome incoming.<br /><br />-Sofia – you’ve been kidnapped by vampires and you’re probably going to die. But that’s okay because the vampire lair is pretty and shiny. HELP.<br /><br />-Nothing about this book appeals to me.<br /><br />-Women are seen as property. Women are not allowed to be anything other than a pretty face and a pair of tits. The vamps are all smirking and ogling, I get it, you don’t need to repeat it every other sentence. Derek ‘owns’ Sofia and doesn’t like it when she speaks out and tries to be bold. NO SHIT. <br /><br />-BUT, ‘I wanted to believe we could still be gentlemen, after all.’ p.45, REALLY. SERIOUSLY. WHAT.<br /><br />-This is just too ridiculous. Let’s snuggle up to the tormented vampire because he poured his undead heart out to me. Oh, Sofia. I despair. <br /><br />-‘In the middle of his performance, it dawned on me that this was exactly the effect Derek Novak had on me: he always managed to – in one way or another – take my breath away.’ p.53 I’m going to get an injury from all this cringing and eye rolling. <br /><br />-Still no redeeming features. The narrative just becomes more ridiculous and unlikable.<br /><br />-‘blood runs thicker than water.’ Technically, yes, blood is indeed the thicker substance, but I still call bullshit on the notion of protecting your murdering rapist of a brother. Funny that. You don’t have to stick by family just because of blood, idiot.<br /><br />-Of course there’s something ‘special’ about Sofia. Seriously, eye rolling so much it hurts. ‘Low latent inhibition.’, honestly this whole thing just makes me want to scoff it’s so poorly done.<br /><br />-Ben appears for the first time as another vamp’s slave. How convenient.<br /><br />-Cringe. Eyeroll. URGH. About as eloquently as I can sum up. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="8220519730394448497" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText3883571412313749468" style="display:none"><b> 3 Stars</b><br><br>First off, I would just like to say: <b>Michael Scofield called, and he would like his mental disorder back!</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1463167120ra/19089422.gif" width="500" height="422" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>There is something to be said about borrowing from the inspiration of shows and books that you yourself enjoy, that I have no issue with. However, not only is one of the scenes basically a carbon-copy of the reveal of Michael’s “gift” in ‘Prison Break’ but it is also something which we are TOLD and not <i>shown</i>. I hope we will see more show of this behaviour in the future because as it stands I don’t see any reason why this was included, other than to tell us what a special snowflake Sofia is. <br><br>This is a fairly typical ya vampire story, which again isn’t a problem, I <b>like</b> vampire stories, even with all their popularity in modern times. While unique in particular ways, the tree villas are a WONDERFUL concept that I truly enjoyed, for the most part this is a pretty standard vampire story. <br><br>We have a beautiful young woman who gets abducted by a vampire, a brooding vampire royal who’s never really been able to cope with the monster he’s become, a couple jealous vampire rivals thrown in to taunt and injure the aforementioned young woman. Voila!<b> Vampires, vampires, everywhere; and too much blood to drink.</b> <br><br>That said, I liked the way the captive/captor scenario played out here, much more than *throat clear* <u>Across the Wine-Dark Sea</u>… because although Sofia is being held against her will, Derek is much more compassionate and empathic in the role as captor. He also does the one thing guaranteed to make me forgive him as a captor <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ which is to let her fucking go when her life is in danger. And not only let <i>her</i> go, but also let her best friend (a boy he is aware she has deep feelings for) go, as well *claps enthusiastically* <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> He has a great deal of lenience for Sofia, and their love arc is a lot easier to relate to; for all it still makes no goddamn sense why a 500 year old vampire would be interested in a 17 year old girl…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1463167120ra/19089423.gif" width="500" height="267" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I will very likely continue this series, at some point, as I found it fairly light and fluffy for the vampire genre. <br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6901237362151767854"><b>4.5 Super romantic, alpha male, oh my goodness stars</b><br/><br/>I’ve seen A Shade of Vampire for years. It’s been on Amazon’s best sellers list forever, but I never picked it up. I realized there is an extended version that has been tweaked and I figured, why not?<br/><br/>As of today there are 22 books in the series, BUT do not fret, only the first 8 books are Sofia’s and Derek’s story. I know I was a bit scared too. I had no expectations getting into this series, I was just in a Young Adult paranormal mood and let </span>
  <span id="freeText6901237362151767854" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Super romantic, alpha male, oh my goodness stars</b><br /><br />I’ve seen A Shade of Vampire for years. It’s been on Amazon’s best sellers list forever, but I never picked it up. I realized there is an extended version that has been tweaked and I figured, why not?<br /><br />As of today there are 22 books in the series, BUT do not fret, only the first 8 books are Sofia’s and Derek’s story. I know I was a bit scared too. I had no expectations getting into this series, I was just in a Young Adult paranormal mood and let me just tell you this.<br /><br />I got well more than I expected. I’m an instant fan. I’m actually kind of happy there are 22 books in the series because I can continually get my fix. <br /><br />This was an easy and fast read. To my surprise it’s filled with romance and the kind of stuff, I crave and swoon over when I pick up these kinds of books. Give me a tortured vampire and a damsel in distress Heroine, yes please!<br /><br />Sofia just turned 18. She’s on vacation with her best friend, Ben, whom she is also in love with. Distraught that Ben kind of ignored her on her birthday, Sofia runs and cries into the night on the beach. That is until she is kidnapped by an evil vampire named Lucas.<br /><br />Let me tell you my thoughts so far… so far, it’s pretty awesome. I really like how the book started and I love that Sofia has a crush on her best friend but then she gets kidnapped into the vampire world?! How cool is that.<br />Lucas is Derek’s brother, so Lucas is the bad guy, but wait, Derek is not such a good guy as well. Well, I didn’t want a likeable Hero. I mean, don’t get me wrong, I LOVE Derek, but he’s a vampire, so he’s also broody and very moody and loves human blood.<br /><br />I love starting a new paranormal book because you get sucked into a whole new world. You learn about the new rules and what other supernatural elements there are. Sofia is Derek’s “slave” and he doesn’t even know what he wants to do with her, but he wants her near. Sofia is desperate to go back home, but she’s super drawn to Derek. Did I forget to mention Derek is a PRINCE! Yeah I know it gets better and better.<br /><br />Tons of stuff happens in this book, it’s short, sweet and pack full of romantic elements. I’m so glad to be starting this new series. <br /><br /><i>Read on Kindle Unlimited</i><br /></span>

<div id="review_522641551" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Erin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4979538-erin"><img alt="Erin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520654483p2/4979538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/522641551?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erin" href="/user/show/4979538-erin">Erin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=romance-erotica-faves">romance-erotica-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=autographed-books">autographed-books</a>
          </div>
