        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer522641551" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15570421378462183823">This book totally took me by surprise, in a good way! With a brave and determined heroine, sexy vampire brothers with a bitter rivalry that is shaping their fate (mmm, hello Damon and Stefan..*sigh*), and a war brewing behind the scenes that is sure to bring suspense and thrills, this is definitely a series to watch. Add to that a beautiful romance that leaves you gasping for more as the first book comes to a close, and I AM HOOKED! <br/><br/><b> "Every second that kiss lasted was another second meant for th</b></span>
  <span id="freeText15570421378462183823" style="display:none">This book totally took me by surprise, in a good way! With a brave and determined heroine, sexy vampire brothers with a bitter rivalry that is shaping their fate (mmm, hello Damon and Stefan..*sigh*), and a war brewing behind the scenes that is sure to bring suspense and thrills, this is definitely a series to watch. Add to that a beautiful romance that leaves you gasping for more as the first book comes to a close, and I AM HOOKED! <br><br><b> "Every second that kiss lasted was another second meant for the truth to sink in. <i> I've already stopped even thinking or dreaming of a life that didn't have Derek Novak in it. </i>"~Sofia </b><br><br>What I loved about this book was that it wasn't a predictable vampire romance storyline. We don't see the sexy hero first, the heroine doesn't fall head over heels for his sparkly skin the minute their eyes meet, and the danger, rather than from other creatures or the humans that hunt them, is from within. In fact, our first glimpse into the world of Bella Forrest's vampires is the tempting morsel himself, older brother Lucas of the Novak family of vamps. He's cruel, selfish, and abusive of his power, and he's destined to wreak havoc as this series moves forward!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407579i/796242._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But despite the evil that Lucas represents, he is still the brother to beautiful Viviene and the gorgeous, troubled Derek (not exactly a name from the 1500s, but I digress), the vampire destined to bring change to their kind. He took a 400 year-long nap to try and avoid it, but he's back and knows what is resting on his shoulders. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407579i/796243.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And just like in the fairy tales, a kiss of true love will be the beginning of it all. Beautiful Sofia, captured and kept prisoner on their island of vampires and human slaves, found herself just as mesmerized by the great Derek as he was of her.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379782540i/434143.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved Derek and Sofia's relationship, it was allowed to grow slowly and show how they began to fall for each other despite her obvious reasons for wanting to hate him. With Lucas looming as a constant threat to her safety, I couldn't help but wish Derek would just throw caution to the wind and play on that awesome chemistry between them! It was a sweet but passionate romance even though he was holding back for her sake; by the time the end rolled around and I was blown over by a heart-wrenching moment and the twist that left me screaming...let's just say I'm going to be very impatient for the next book!!! <br><br>Overall, great new vampire series with captivating characters and a storyline that's sure to keep readers hooked for the long haul!<br></span>

  <span id="freeText17580043528941655602" style="display:none">I found A SHADE OF VAMPIRE thanks to Amazon recommendations, it had over 600 five-star ratings, and it was a mere $.99 for Kindle. I was kinda excited to find something new.<br /><br />It was a trap.<br /><br />Our main POV first-person narrators are Sofia and Derek. Sofia is our red-haired, green-eyed young woman vacationing with a friend's family when she's abducted on the night of her 17th birthday. Derek is the 500 year old vampire prince just woken from a four century slumber and given his own harem of beautiful human women, of whom Sofia is included.<br /><br />If I could go deeper into plot and character, I would. If I could. A SHADE is exactly what it sounds like: an unimaginative Mary Sue wish fulfillment fantasy with amateur prose and trite dialogue. The story is predictable simply because there isn't anything more to it than what I mentioned above.<br /><br />So Derek and Sofia are thrown together and for some unknown reason they intrigue each other. No reason, really. Even though we do get a lot of sappy contrived interactions between them. Sofia doesn't seem afraid for her life, even if she does make a token escape attempt. She adjusts to her new role as slave pretty easily.<br /><br />Derek doesn't seem like a vampire other than he craves blood and is strong, which makes the vampire culture really bland. Why is Derek a vampire prince? Because of some vaguely explained thing he did five hundred years ago. So who's been in charge for the 400 years he's been asleep? Why does Derek not seem to have an occupation although they talk about getting rid of those pesky hunters? And why are vampires holding so much stock in a prophecy? (Why do fantasy writers still use such contrived methods to create tension?) I don't know.<br /><br />They spend the book at this vampire sanctuary Derek's family built while he was sleeping. It's some island (no idea where) with beautiful forests, and because of a witch it exists in perpetual night. How do the trees stay living after 400 years of perpetual night? Why would vampires feel the need to build penthouse apartments in redwood and sequoia trees? Why mention no ladders/stairs to the penthouses but Sofia can get to the ground somehow? Why end it with a confusing cliffhanger? I don't know.<br /><br />Why are there no answers to these questions? Because I don't think the author knows the answers to them, either. The prose is amateurish, the dialogue is expositional yet tells me nothing, the descriptions are ham-handed and lack originality. If anything, A SHADE OF VAMPIRE is a warning lesson to all you wannabe authors out there: please, no more novels like this to waste my time.<br /><br />Recommended Age: Um, I suppose it's aimed at a teenage audience who are fans of TWILIGHT, but you don't want your kids rotting their brains by reading this drek<br />Language: None<br />Violence: So lame it's a comedy<br />Sex: Referenced<br /><br />*** Find this and other reviews at Elitist Book Reviews. ***</span>
  <a data-text-id="17580043528941655602" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1510762730" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1510762730" />
    <a title="Hannah ◇Reader in the Rough◇" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/42354688-hannah-reader-in-the-rough"><img alt="Hannah ◇Reader in the Rough◇" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589491925p2/42354688.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1510762730?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hannah ◇Reader in the Rough◇" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hannah ◇Reader in the Rough◇" href="/user/show/42354688-hannah-reader-in-the-rough">Hannah ◇Reader in the Rough◇</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of Jennifer L. Amentrout</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42354688-hannah-reader-in-the-rough?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1510762730" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5792598343701715569"><i> "She was the most beautiful to behold— not because her appearance drew me in above and beyond the others.<br/> <br/>No. <br/><br/>She was beautiful because, at a time when she had every right to be terrified, she managed to show comfort to another person who needed it. The moment she’d grabbed the hand of the girl beside her, all the others had paled in comparison. She showed me a humanity I longed to return to. <br/><br/>But I was the predator." </i><br/><br/><br/><b> 2.5 Stars. Not Bad. </b><br/><br/>Is this as good as Vampire Academy? No. Is it as terrible</span>
  <span id="freeText5792598343701715569" style="display:none"><i> "She was the most beautiful to behold— not because her appearance drew me in above and beyond the others.<br /> <br />No. <br /><br />She was beautiful because, at a time when she had every right to be terrified, she managed to show comfort to another person who needed it. The moment she’d grabbed the hand of the girl beside her, all the others had paled in comparison. She showed me a humanity I longed to return to. <br /><br />But I was the predator." </i><br /><br /><br /><b> 2.5 Stars. Not Bad. </b><br /><br />Is this as good as Vampire Academy? No. Is it as terrible as New Moon? No.<br /><br />On that scale this would be along the lines of Jennifer L Amentrout. It's vampire-lite. The pages turn fast, and the story is easy to wrap around.<br /><br /><b>What I like: </b><br /><br />1) Sofia is a "different girl". But instead of just claiming it, we actually get a reasonable medical diagnosis as to why. <br /><br />2) The comaraderie between the girls in the "harem". Instead of uber bitchy stuff, they band together. <br /><br />3) Derek. I'm not in love, he is no Demitri or Adrian, but he is interesting and thoughtful and not an old jackass.<br /><br />4) It doesn't make my brain hurt. It is the equivalent to punch at a party. It has no kick, but why not!? It's a great filler read. Like Lays potato chips before dinner (I snack before dinner).<br /><br /><b>Didn't like: </b><br /><br />1)Lack of worldbuilding. (spoilery: it expands on the world and history in the second book)<br /><br />2) Ben... ugh. Modelesque boy that Sofia loves for reasons unbeknownst to me. I hate the scenes with them<br /><br />3) The harem thing isn't utilized, like at all. It's more a prop as opposed to a plot point.<br /><br />This is more a prequel than anything. Albeit a shitty, nondescript one. A prequel should set the stage. This does not. It feels like I'm viewing a dress rehearsal. And yes, there's insta-attraction, but it was handled well, in my opinion.<br /><br />We'll see if book two works out these issues. <b>Yes, I thought it was good enough to read on. :)</b><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />Original comments: Just saw an article on Facebook hailing this as the next "Twilight"... Now I'm afraid to touch it. It's free on kindle unlimited, though. Decisions, decisions...</span>
  <a data-text-id="5792598343701715569" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=supernatural">supernatural</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=november-challenge-2018">november-challenge-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2586152105" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7281420255549856515"><b>Ya know... pretty good. </b><br/><br/>Maybe it's because <i>A Shade of Vampire</i> reminded me of some vampy tv shows but I ended up liking this book. It was definitely fast paces, but that might've just been me and my sprinting. <br/><br/>In this book, you will meet Sofia. She's at a party one night and something happens between her and her best friend Ben. I guess they were going to take their relationship to the next level.. but it never happened. Well, she walks out crying and ends up at the beach. From there, she runs in</span>
  <span id="freeText7281420255549856515" style="display:none"><b>Ya know... pretty good. </b><br /><br />Maybe it's because <i>A Shade of Vampire</i> reminded me of some vampy tv shows but I ended up liking this book. It was definitely fast paces, but that might've just been me and my sprinting. <br /><br />In this book, you will meet Sofia. She's at a party one night and something happens between her and her best friend Ben. I guess they were going to take their relationship to the next level.. but it never happened. Well, she walks out crying and ends up at the beach. From there, she runs into Lucas. UGH LUCAS - I hate him so freaking much! <br /><br />The next day (maybe) she wakes up. She's been kidnapped and she is thrown into this vampire harem for the waking prince. Once he awakes.. he looks into her mesmerizing eyes and basically says no to the harem and just wants her. It was interesting to see that happen and I wanted to know more about them.<br /><br />WELL, I liked Derek and Sofia. They were cute and adorable. I'm just waiting for something to happen, like other than that kiss I got at the end. I want more from them. They got closer throughout this book - which, if I'm being honest would've probably happened to anyone that was kidnapped and constantly has their life threatened. AGAIN, UGH LUCAS!<br /><br />I totally called that ending though but I also can't wait to dive into the next book.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11960842818949111718">Bella is one of my favourite Authors.<br/>Book 1 is a little slow to start with as she is building up the scene of the shade and the characters. <br/><br/>Hang on in there as her books only get better and better.<br/><br/>This book is nothing like twilight it's so much more than that which you will become to see once you get into the book.<br/><br/>Bella has a way of absorbing you into the shade.   <span id="freeText11960842818949111718" style="display:none">Bella is one of my favourite Authors.<br />Book 1 is a little slow to start with as she is building up the scene of the shade and the characters. <br /><br />Hang on in there as her books only get better and better.<br /><br />This book is nothing like twilight it's so much more than that which you will become to see once you get into the book.<br /><br />Bella has a way of absorbing you into the shade. I truly feel like I have been on a personal journey with every one of her characters.<br /><br />The shade is a magical island where vampires live protected from the human world under a darkness spell cast by the witch within the shade. She places a protection spell on the island so it becomes invisible to hunters and humans.<br />As you know vampires are not immune from daylight.<br /><br />To begin with you see Humans are kept as slaves but one special lady Sophia is slowly changing vampire ways with her charm. <br /><br />Derek Novak is a strong vampire &amp; is not to be tested. However Sophia has a way of melting even the coldest of hearts.<br /><br />Please give the Shade a go &amp; don't give up as it really does get better &amp; better.<br /><br />I'm currently reading book 28.</span>

<div id="review_654629584" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/654629584" />
    <a title="Camila (previously the opinionated Catruler)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18091208-camila-previously-the-opinionated-catruler"><img alt="Camila (previously the opinionated Catruler)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460588276p2/18091208.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/654629584?book_show_action=true">Jun 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Camila (previously the opinionated Catruler)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Camila (previously the opinionated Catruler)" href="/user/show/18091208-camila-previously-the-opinionated-catruler">Camila (previously the opinionated Catruler)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18091208-camila-previously-the-opinionated-catruler?shelf=dnf">dnf</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer654629584" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6788912260727430941">  It was only 149 pages long, but I gave up at the 30%.<br/><br/>  I am so incredibly sorry. I really am. A couple of months ago I entered a giveaway to win this book, which I did not do. However, the author approached me with the opportunity to read it in exchange of an <b>honest</b> review. Well, the honest to Rowling truth is that the book (what I read) bored me. The writing wasn't necessarily bad, and maybe if I had continued the story and characters would have gotten better. <u>I SWEAR I tried</u>, I really did. B</span>
  <span id="freeText6788912260727430941" style="display:none">  It was only 149 pages long, but I gave up at the 30%.<br /><br />  I am so incredibly sorry. I really am. A couple of months ago I entered a giveaway to win this book, which I did not do. However, the author approached me with the opportunity to read it in exchange of an <b>honest</b> review. Well, the honest to Rowling truth is that the book (what I read) bored me. The writing wasn't necessarily bad, and maybe if I had continued the story and characters would have gotten better. <u>I SWEAR I tried</u>, I really did. But what's the point in reading a book that's simply not for you? Or maybe it wasn't the time. Anyway, I just didn't really enjoy it.<br /><br />  If you want the specifics, the two main characters were whiny people (or vamp) who tried too hard. At least Cinderella's Prince wasn't that broody. They were physically perfect for each other, and had insta-love. I dare you tell me that wasn't completely unrealistic and irrational. He was violating her, yet it didn't feel that way for her. He had always had drinking problems, but the moment she speaks a few words he gets over his urge. I've been known to love cases of insta-attraction, sometimes not even seeing it as that until someone mentioned it. This was just too much.<br /><br />  The world-building had potential, and yet I was once again bored by how it was presented. Not one for info dumps. Not one for insta-love. Not one for cheesy writing. Not one for a quick pace that feels slow. I'm just not the girl for this book, but you might me.<br /><br />  I want to truthfully thank Bella Forrest for giving me the chance. Possibly the wrong chick, sorry about that.<br /><br />- <a href="http://aliveorundead.blogspot.com.ar/" rel="nofollow noopener">Alive or Undead</a> ~ 2013 -</span>
  <a data-text-id="6788912260727430941" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer189575833806666653"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398857ra/771197.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I love a good vampire story. The power, the darkness, the badass men... it all just works for me. Now I would choose a shifter over a vamp if i ever got a choice but a girl has to keep her options open so I am always willing to entertain the thought a hot vamper ;) <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397936ra/768468.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Derek for me is a little like Eric Northman; He loves what is his, he thinks about/is into being more mainstream/working with the humans instead of just thinking they are all food, he is in a position of power, he feels little to no r</span>
  <span id="freeText189575833806666653" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398857ra/771197.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I love a good vampire story. The power, the darkness, the badass men... it all just works for me. Now I would choose a shifter over a vamp if i ever got a choice but a girl has to keep her options open so I am always willing to entertain the thought a hot vamper ;) <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397936ra/768468.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Derek for me is a little like Eric Northman; He loves what is his, he thinks about/is into being more mainstream/working with the humans instead of just thinking they are all food, he is in a position of power, he feels little to no regret for drinking/eating/hurting people that disagree with him/get in his way/want to hurt him/try to hurt what is his. In short Derek is a loveable bad boy with some swoon appeal. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380787538ra/3122750.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Sofia Claremont is a slightly naive 17 year old girl, who is gorgeous &amp; a lovely friendly person. Everyone she meets seems to crush on her (even the girls seem to develop a girl crush on her). She was a little too.. sweet (if that is the right word) at times for me but I still liked her &amp; thought she was a cool character. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380787538ra/3122751.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The story is quite short, it seemed like I had just started reading &amp; it was already over - but! that is also because I got really engrossed in the story &amp; did not put it down. Bad stuff happens, there are surprises, there is a love connection, there is clearly more install for all the characters and there is a cliff hanger ending. <br>Good news is the book is super cheap, the series is already at book 4 and book five is coming out soon so there is no reason not to pick it up! <br>I have read a few reviews for the next books in the series and apparently the books get even better. I am away to start book 2 now so I will let you know what i think. </span>

        rated it

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15922517-maria-dimitrova?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2121835294" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16692028197340258522">One day, many months ago, in a fit of insanity I got this while it was on some sort of a sale. And today I had some free time. So I though "Why the hell not". And while it was not awful it was definitely boring. And flat. And I couldn't muster any sympathy for Sofia. Or any feeling other than mild disgust about Derek. So I know I won't pick up the rest of the series. Especially seeing as to how many of them there are. I guess I really am too old for YA.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jSjx96jVMYvGmxY8SYzgKBxmnwV1Bf7t72NhuePhhqHruGl7VB3Njs0lkq9y/Di3lssZQlDyWNXl+7EUmaUcuw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('U8mBxIDbwK7e65oS5sFWsuC6Q+9fL40mpOHA0dJe+pI1WRlIfBM8q9VVHoHdsY4tahfFqHrYKx6ueRB8qBpgiA==')})
  }
//]]>

He’d been her light in a lifetime of darkness. Six years ago, that darkness stole him away.
